darasal 2002 main hyderabad neshnal games ke liye sports village banane vaali IVRCL karzon or nuksaan se buree tarah ghiri hui he
 The company has a debt of about 10,000 crores
 2015 disambar main iskaa ghaataa 2000 karod kaa ho gaya he
 The company wanted to increase the cost of construction of the bridge
 kiskaa daawa sahi-sahi or kiskaa galat yah kahana mushkil he lekin pul girane se 25 logon ko apni jaan jarur ganvaani padi he
 8 people of the company have been arrested in Kolkata, but they should not be spared if there is a government authority responsible for delay in construction of the bridge
 tippaniyan Now come to today's question
 kya fliover itane jaruri hai ki ham kahin bhi kaise bhi bana dete hai

 chote shaharon main kuch fliowaron ko dekhakar to ji ghabara hi jaataa he

 netaa bhi logon ko aashwast karne ke liye pliover kii aadharshila rakh dete hai
 In Delhi, in the last ten-fifteen years, close to a hundred flyovers would have been built
 is shahar ke anubhav se bataa saktaa hum ki kuch fliover to kaamyaab lagate hai lekin zyaadaatar fliover ke banane ke baad bhi jam kii samasya samaapt nahin hoti he

 bengalooru main 40 fliover ban gaye hai

 aae din akhabaaron main fliover ke shilanyas or udghaatan kii tasviren aap dekhte rahete hai lekin kya kabhi dekha he ki inase trephic kii samasya dur hoti bhi he yaa nahin

 paryaavaran par bhi asar hota hi hoga
 Do you also think that the traffic jam problem has ended since the flyover came
 mere khud ke anubhav main to donon hi baaten hai

 kisi sookhe naale kii tarah donon taraf ke makaanon se sate yah fliover bahata chalaa aa rahaa he, badrang, benur or beong

 na samaj, na kalpana dikhti he

 pul yahaan ke makaanon ko chhukar guzar rahaa he

 ek foot kaa bhi antar nahin he

 kam se paanch se chah foot kaa antar to rakhega

 ab aap bataaie yah pul ban jaataa to yahaan ke makaanon par kya asar padataa

 logon ne mukadmaa bhi kiya hua he

 ) afghanistan ke ek ballebaaj ne first class cricket kaa ek anokhaa record apane naam kiya he
 18-year-old Bahir Shah, batting brilliantly in his first four first-class matches, 207
 75 ke everej se 831 ran bana chuke hai
 Talking of scoring the most runs in the first four matches of the first class career, Bashir has surpassed Australian legend Bill Ponsford
 ponsford ne apane shuruaati itane hi maichon main 741 ran banaae the
 First Class Cricket: Bahir Shah's opening 4 matches First match - Double centuries in debut (256 *) Third match - Centuries in both innings (111 and 116) Fourth match - Triple century (303 *) After Rashid, now Bauheer Shah has shocked Shouyyarashid Khan
 After Bahir Shah has caught the attention of the cricket world
 apni sateek gugali se pahchaan banane vaale raashid khan ne 2015 main tii-20 international or vanade interneshal main debyue kiya tha
 He was 17 at the time
 raashid ne 29 vanade main abtak 63 wicket or 27 tii-20 international main 42 wicket nikaale hai
 He took 7 wickets for 18 against June West Indies
 unka yah pradarshan vanade itihaas kii chauthi sarvshereshth gendbaaji he
 Last week, when industry and politics were chewing nails in wait for the first full budget of Modi government, many more budgets were also being presented in the country
 bharat ek bajet kaa nahin balki 29 bajaton kaa desh he or rajyon ke in 29 bajaton ko behad gambhirtha se lene kaa vakt aa gaya he
 In the next one year, the states of India will be equipped with the financial power, which will change not only the economic policies but also the face of politics in the country
 francisi lekhak victor hugo kehete the, us vichaar ko koi nahin roak saktaa jiskaa samay aa gaya ho
 The time had come for states to be given the freedom and resources to make economic decisions so it could not be stopped
 ise aap bharat kaa sabase doorgaami aarthik sudhaar kah sakate hai jo pichley ek dashak kii siyaasi chillpon ke bich chupchaap aa jamaa he
 Before Narendra Modi came to power, the Finance Commission had started the journey to increase the financial powers of the states, Modi abolished the Planning Commission and brought it to the destination
 modi sarkaar ke pehle purna bajet ke saath bharat main sanghavaad kaa ek nayaa khaakaa ubhar rahaa he, jisamen shakti sampann centre ab kamjor hoga jabaki rajya vittiya maamalon main nai takat banenge or vikaas kaa takaza ab keval dilli se nahin balki jaipur, bhopal, lakhanu, chennai, bengaluru, kolkata se bhi hoga, jinhen is nai vittiya takat va aazaadee ko sanbhaalane kii kshamtaayen viksit kerani hai
 Even after listening to Jaitley's speech, are you unaware of these things? Narendra Modi may not be able to clarify the new blueprint of decentralized economic policy planning by abolishing the Planning Commission, but he must end the dominance of the center in the sharing of economic resources gave
 bachaa hua kaam chaudaaven vitt ayog ne kar diya he
 The government has accepted its report before the budget, it is going to change the map of financial relations between the center and the states
 rajyon ko kendriya karon main ab 42 fisadi hissaa milegaa yani pichley formule se 10 fisadi zyada
 The central government will give them funds without wrapping them in terms and not only this, a new formula for sharing the share of resources of the central state will also be implemented which is made by looking at the modern needs
 kendriya karon main milane vaala hissaa 2016 ke baad kareeb 1
 76 trillion Rs
 bad jayega
 One lakh crores to the states from the allocation of coal mines
 mil rahe hai
 Grants and funds from the Planning Commission will also increase and GST will also increase the earnings of the states
 baat sirf vittiya sansadhano kii supplai kii nahin he
 In light of the farewell of the Planning Commission and the recommendations of the Finance Commission, the states are also getting sufficient freedom to spend these resources, which is also a big challenge

 lekin samasya yah he ki tex main sarkaar agar ek rupee kii bhi kami karti he to uske khajaane main salanaa 13,000 karod rupee kaa nuksaan hota he

 75 per liter! Another option is to bring fuel to GST

 75 per liter

 bharat, japan or china un asian deshon main shaamil hai, jo opek deshon se kachche tel kii kharid ke liye oonchi keemat dete hai

 yah dastur saal 1987 se chal rahaa he
